PathOfExileClipboardListener
============================

Clipboard Listener and Stash Manager for Path of Exile

To use this you will need a database called PathOfExile on a SQL Server instance called EXILE, i.e. localhost\EXILE.

Once the database has been created the following script will create and populate the objects:

USE [PathOfExile]
GO
/****** Object:  Table [dbo].[CharacterClass]    Script Date: 01/23/2014 23:41:04 ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
SET ANSI_PADDING ON
GO
CREATE TABLE [dbo].[CharacterClass](
	[CharacterClassId] [int] NOT NULL,
	[CharacterClassName] [varchar](50) NULL,
 CONSTRAINT [pk$CharacterClass] PRIMARY KEY CLUSTERED 
(
	[CharacterClassId] ASC
)WITH (PAD_INDEX  = OFF, STATISTICS_NORECOMPUTE  = OFF, IGNORE_DUP_KEY = OFF, ALLOW_ROW_LOCKS  = ON, ALLOW_PAGE_LOCKS  = ON) ON [PRIMARY]
) ON [PRIMARY]
GO
SET ANSI_PADDING OFF
GO

CREATE TABLE [dbo].[Character](
	[CharacterId] [uniqueidentifier] NOT NULL,
	[CharacterClassId] [int] NULL,
	[CharacterName] [varchar](50) NULL,
	[CharacterLevel] [int] NULL,
	[LeagueId] [uniqueidentifier] NULL,
	[EquipHelmet] [uniqueidentifier] NULL,
	[EquipBodyArmour] [uniqueidentifier] NULL,
	[EquipGloves] [uniqueidentifier] NULL,
	[EquipBoots] [uniqueidentifier] NULL,
	[EquipBelt] [uniqueidentifier] NULL,
	[EquipRRing] [uniqueidentifier] NULL,
	[EquipLRing] [uniqueidentifier] NULL,
	[EquipAmulet] [uniqueidentifier] NULL,
	[EquipLHand] [uniqueidentifier] NULL,
	[EquipRHand] [uniqueidentifier] NULL,
 CONSTRAINT [pk$Character] PRIMARY KEY CLUSTERED 
(
	[CharacterId] ASC
)WITH (PAD_INDEX  = OFF, STATISTICS_NORECOMPUTE  = OFF, IGNORE_DUP_KEY = OFF, ALLOW_ROW_LOCKS  = ON, ALLOW_PAGE_LOCKS  = ON) ON [PRIMARY]
) ON [PRIMARY]
GO
SET ANSI_PADDING OFF
GO

/****** Object:  Table [dbo].[Mod]    Script Date: 01/23/2014 23:41:04 ******/

SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON

CREATE TABLE [dbo].[Mod](
	[ModId] [int] NOT NULL,
	[ModName] [varchar](100) NULL,
	[ModRealName] [varchar](100) NULL,
	[ModPair] [int] NULL,
	[Armour] [int] NULL,
	[Weapons] [int] NULL,
	[Jewellery] [int] NULL,
 CONSTRAINT [pk$Mod] PRIMARY KEY CLUSTERED 
(
	[ModId] ASC
)WITH (PAD_INDEX  = OFF, STATISTICS_NORECOMPUTE  = OFF, IGNORE_DUP_KEY = OFF, ALLOW_ROW_LOCKS  = ON, ALLOW_PAGE_LOCKS  = ON) ON [PRIMARY],
 CONSTRAINT [uq$ModKey] UNIQUE NONCLUSTERED 
(
	[ModRealName] ASC,
	[Weapons] ASC,
	[Armour] ASC,
	[Jewellery] ASC,
	[ModPair] ASC
)WITH (PAD_INDEX  = OFF, STATISTICS_NORECOMPUTE  = OFF, IGNORE_DUP_KEY = OFF, ALLOW_ROW_LOCKS  = ON, ALLOW_PAGE_LOCKS  = ON) ON [PRIMARY],
 CONSTRAINT [uq$ModName] UNIQUE NONCLUSTERED 
(
	[ModName] ASC
)WITH (PAD_INDEX  = OFF, STATISTICS_NORECOMPUTE  = OFF, IGNORE_DUP_KEY = OFF, ALLOW_ROW_LOCKS  = ON, ALLOW_PAGE_LOCKS  = ON) ON [PRIMARY]
) ON [PRIMARY]
GO
SET ANSI_PADDING OFF
GO

	[BaseItemId] [int] NOT NULL,
	[ItemName] [varchar](255) NULL,
	[ItemTypeId] [int] NOT NULL,

	[Evasion] [int] NULL,
	[EnergyShield] [int] NULL,
	[DamagePhysicalMin] [int] NULL,

	[Mod1ValueMax] [int] NULL,

	[Mod2ValueMin] [int] NULL,
	[Mod2ValueMax] [int] NULL,
